following: " "NOMENCLATURE CONVENTIONS The conventions used for establishing INCI names are as follows: 1.
Traditional stems are retained as combining forms when consistent with other systems (see rule 17). 6.
Straight-chain alkyl groups are described by their common stem names (see rule 17). 14.
Ethylhexyl myristate, Cetyl ethylhexanoate, Diethylhexylamine, Triethylhexanoin, Butyloctanoic acid). 16.

The term "monium" describes a monomethyl-substituted quaternary nitrogen; "dimonium" describes a dimethyl-subsituted quaternary nitrogen; "trimonium" describes a trimethyl-substituted quaternary nitrogen. 23.
In the event that chemical names are very complex, a colour/number combination is used prefixed by the letters "HC". 29.
The following references are used to establish the LinnÃ©-derived for botanicals: (a) The primary referece is Penso, G., Index Plantarum Medicinalium Totius Mundi Eorumque Synonymorum, O.E.M.F.
Kathon CG: Aqua, Chloromethylisothiazolinone, Methylisothiazolinone, Magnesium chloride, Magnesium nitrate). 33.
Because names based on the approximate molecular weight of the ethylene oxide polymer are also in common use, the following table is provided to allow easy conversion between the two systems: Approximate Molecular Weight | Average Number of Monomer Units | 100 | 2 | 200 | 4 | 300 | 6 | 400 | 8 | 450 | 9 | 500 | 10 | 600 | 12 | 1000 | 20 | 1540 | 32 | 1800 | 36 | 2000 | 40 | 3000 | 60 | 4000 | 75 | 6000 | 150 | 8000 | 180 | 36.
Other propoxylated substances are named accordingly. 37.
The term "Pareth" applies to ethoxylated parffinic alcohols containing both even- and odd-carbon chain length fractions. 39.
The term "Poloxamer" denotes a symmetrical block copolymer formed by ethoxylation of polypropylene glycol.
The term "Meroxapol" denotes a symmetrical clock copolymer formed by the propoxylation of polyethlene glycol.
The term "Poloxamine" denotes a symmetrical block copolymer formed by successively propoxylating then ethoxylating ethylene diamine.
Copolymers of ethylene glycol and propylene glycol which do not form symmetrical block copolymers are named as PEG/PPG-X/Y derivatives where X and Y are the average number of ethylene oxide and propylene oxide monomer units respectively. 46.
When the name is: | the alkyl is: | octoxynol | tetramethylbutyl | nonoxynol | nonyl | dodoxynol | dodecyl | pentadoxynol | pentadecyl | 47.
The term "Ceramide" as part of an INCI name will be assigned to those classes and structures of natural lipids derived from skin as reported by Wertz P.W., Miethke M.C., Long S.A., Strauss J.M.
Synthetic peptides consisting of more than 100 amino acids are designated by the term polypeptide, followed by an arbitrary number.
The amino acid residues may include the following: Alanine | Glutamine | Phenylalanine | Arginine | Glycine | Proline | Asparagine | Histidine | Serine | Aspartic Acid | Isoleucine | Threonine | Cysteine | Leucine | Tryptophan | Cystine | Lysine | Tyrosine | Glutamic Acid | Methionine | Valine | 51.
